<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.07</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders.</p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">The Annual Meeting of Shareholders of Apple Inc. was held on February&#160;23, 2021. At the Annual Meeting, Apple&#8217;s shareholders voted on the following five proposals and cast their votes as described below.</p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
